9 /// This pass custom lowers llvm.gather and llvm.scatter instructions to ----
10 /// arm.mve.gather and arm.mve.scatter intrinsics, optimising the code to ----
11 /// produce a better final result as we go. ----

171 bool MVEGatherScatterLowering::isLegalTypeAndAlignment(unsigned NumElements, 0
172 unsigned ElemSize, ----
173 Align Alignment) { ----
174 if (((NumElements == 4 && 0
175 (ElemSize == 32 || ElemSize == 16 || ElemSize == 8)) || 0
176 (NumElements == 8 && (ElemSize == 16 || ElemSize == 8)) || 0
177 (NumElements == 16 && ElemSize == 8)) && 0
178 Alignment >= ElemSize / 8) 0
179 return true; 0
180 LLVM_DEBUG(dbgs() << "masked gathers/scatters: instruction does not have " 0
181 << "valid alignment or vector type \n"); ----
182 return false; 0
183 } ----
184 ----
185 static bool checkOffsetSize(Value *Offsets, unsigned TargetElemCount) { 0
186 // Offsets that are not of type are sign extended by the ----
187 // getelementptr instruction, and MVE gathers/scatters treat the offset as ----
188 // unsigned. Thus, if the element size is smaller than 32, we can only allow ----
189 // positive offsets - i.e., the offsets are not allowed to be variables we ----
190 // can't look into. ----
191 // Additionally, offsets have to either originate from a zext of a ----
192 // vector with element types smaller or equal the type of the gather we're ----
193 // looking at, or consist of constants that we can check are small enough ----
194 // to fit into the gather type. ----
195 // Thus we check that 0 < value < 2^TargetElemSize. ----
196 unsigned TargetElemSize = 128 / TargetElemCount; 0
197 unsigned OffsetElemSize = cast(Offsets->getType()) 0
198 ->getElementType() ----
199 ->getScalarSizeInBits(); 0
200 if (OffsetElemSize != TargetElemSize || OffsetElemSize != 32) { 0
201 Constant *ConstOff = dyn_cast(Offsets); 0
202 if (!ConstOff) 0
203 return false; 0
204 int64_t TargetElemMaxSize = (1ULL << TargetElemSize); 0
205 auto CheckValueSize = [TargetElemMaxSize](Value *OffsetElem) { 0
206 ConstantInt *OConst = dyn_cast(OffsetElem); 0
207 if (!OConst) 0
208 return false; 0
209 int SExtValue = OConst->getSExtValue(); 0
210 if (SExtValue >= TargetElemMaxSize || SExtValue < 0) 0
211 return false; 0
212 return true; 0
213 }; 0
214 if (isa(ConstOff->getType())) { 0
215 for (unsigned i = 0; i < TargetElemCount; i++) { 0
216 if (!CheckValueSize(ConstOff->getAggregateElement(i))) 0
217 return false; 0
218 } ----
219 } else { ----
220 if (!CheckValueSize(ConstOff)) 0
221 return false; 0
222 } ----
223 } ----
224 return true; 0
225 } ----
226 ----
227 Value *MVEGatherScatterLowering::decomposePtr(Value *Ptr, Value *&Offsets, 0
228 int &Scale, FixedVectorType *Ty, ----
229 Type *MemoryTy, ----
230 IRBuilder<> &Builder) { ----
231 if (auto *GEP = dyn_cast(Ptr)) { 0
232 if (Value *V = decomposeGEP(Offsets, Ty, GEP, Builder)) { 0
233 Scale = 0
234 computeScale(GEP->getSourceElementType()->getPrimitiveSizeInBits(), 0
235 MemoryTy->getScalarSizeInBits()); ----
236 return Scale == -1 ? nullptr : V; 0
237 } ----
238 } ----
239 ----
240 // If we couldn't use the GEP (or it doesn't exist), attempt to use a ----
241 // BasePtr of 0 with Ptr as the Offsets, so long as there are only 4 ----
242 // elements. ----
243 FixedVectorType *PtrTy = cast(Ptr->getType()); 0
244 if (PtrTy->getNumElements() != 4 || MemoryTy->getScalarSizeInBits() == 32) 0
245 return nullptr; 0
246 Value *Zero = ConstantInt::get(Builder.getInt32Ty(), 0); 0
247 Value *BasePtr = Builder.CreateIntToPtr(Zero, Builder.getInt8PtrTy()); 0
248 Offsets = Builder.CreatePtrToInt( 0
249 Ptr, FixedVectorType::get(Builder.getInt32Ty(), 4)); 0
250 Scale = 0; 0
251 return BasePtr; 0
252 } ----
253 ----
254 Value *MVEGatherScatterLowering::decomposeGEP(Value *&Offsets, 0
255 FixedVectorType *Ty, ----
256 GetElementPtrInst *GEP, ----
257 IRBuilder<> &Builder) { ----
258 if (!GEP) { 0
259 LLVM_DEBUG(dbgs() << "masked gathers/scatters: no getelementpointer " 0
260 << "found\n"); ----
261 return nullptr; 0
262 } ----
263 LLVM_DEBUG(dbgs() << "masked gathers/scatters: getelementpointer found." 0
264 << " Looking at intrinsic for base + vector of offsets\n"); ----
265 Value *GEPPtr = GEP->getPointerOperand(); 0
266 Offsets = GEP->getOperand(1); 0
267 if (GEPPtr->getType()->isVectorTy() || 0
268 !isa(Offsets->getType())) 0
269 return nullptr; 0
270 ----
271 if (GEP->getNumOperands() != 2) { 0
272 LLVM_DEBUG(dbgs() << "masked gathers/scatters: getelementptr with too many" 0
273 << " operands. Expanding.\n"); ----
274 return nullptr; 0
275 } ----
276 Offsets = GEP->getOperand(1); 0
277 unsigned OffsetsElemCount = ----
278 cast(Offsets->getType())->getNumElements(); 0
279 // Paranoid check whether the number of parallel lanes is the same ----
280 assert(Ty->getNumElements() == OffsetsElemCount); 0
281 ----
282 ZExtInst *ZextOffs = dyn_cast(Offsets); 0
283 if (ZextOffs) 0
284 Offsets = ZextOffs->getOperand(0); 0
285 FixedVectorType *OffsetType = cast(Offsets->getType()); 0
286 ----
287 // If the offsets are already being zext-ed to , that relieves us of ----
288 // having to make sure that they won't overflow. ----
289 if (!ZextOffs || cast(ZextOffs->getDestTy()) 0
290 ->getElementType() ----
291 ->getScalarSizeInBits() != 32) 0
292 if (!checkOffsetSize(Offsets, OffsetsElemCount)) 0
293 return nullptr; 0
294 ----
295 // The offset sizes have been checked; if any truncating or zext-ing is ----
296 // required to fix them, do that now ----
297 if (Ty != Offsets->getType()) { 0
298 if ((Ty->getElementType()->getScalarSizeInBits() < 0
299 OffsetType->getElementType()->getScalarSizeInBits())) { 0
300 Offsets = Builder.CreateTrunc(Offsets, Ty); 0
301 } else { ----
302 Offsets = Builder.CreateZExt(Offsets, VectorType::getInteger(Ty)); 0
303 } ----
304 } ----
305 // If none of the checks failed, return the gep's base pointer ----
306 LLVM_DEBUG(dbgs() << "masked gathers/scatters: found correct offsets\n"); 0
307 return GEPPtr; 0
308 } ----
309 ----
310 void MVEGatherScatterLowering::lookThroughBitcast(Value *&Ptr) { 0
311 // Look through bitcast instruction if #elements is the same ----
312 if (auto *BitCast = dyn_cast(Ptr)) { 0
313 auto *BCTy = cast(BitCast->getType()); 0
314 auto *BCSrcTy = cast(BitCast->getOperand(0)->getType()); 0
315 if (BCTy->getNumElements() == BCSrcTy->getNumElements()) { 0
316 LLVM_DEBUG(dbgs() << "masked gathers/scatters: looking through " 0
317 << "bitcast\n"); ----
318 Ptr = BitCast->getOperand(0); 0
319 } ----
320 } ----
321 } 0
322 ----
323 int MVEGatherScatterLowering::computeScale(unsigned GEPElemSize, 0
324 unsigned MemoryElemSize) { ----
325 // This can be a 32bit load/store scaled by 4, a 16bit load/store scaled by 2, ----
326 // or a 8bit, 16bit or 32bit load/store scaled by 1 ----
327 if (GEPElemSize == 32 && MemoryElemSize == 32) 0
328 return 2; 0
329 else if (GEPElemSize == 16 && MemoryElemSize == 16) 0
330 return 1; 0
331 else if (GEPElemSize == 8) 0
332 return 0; 0
333 LLVM_DEBUG(dbgs() << "masked gathers/scatters: incorrect scale. Can't " 0
334 << "create intrinsic\n"); ----
335 return -1; 0
336 } ----
337 ----
338 std::optional MVEGatherScatterLowering::getIfConst(const Value *V) { 0
339 const Constant *C = dyn_cast(V); 0
340 if (C && C->getSplatValue()) 0
341 return std::optional{C->getUniqueInteger().getSExtValue()}; 0
342 if (!isa(V)) 0
343 return std::optional{}; 0
344 ----
345 const Instruction *I = cast(V); 0
346 if (I->getOpcode() == Instruction::Add || I->getOpcode() == Instruction::Or || 0
347 I->getOpcode() == Instruction::Mul || 0
348 I->getOpcode() == Instruction::Shl) { 0
349 std::optional Op0 = getIfConst(I->getOperand(0)); 0
350 std::optional Op1 = getIfConst(I->getOperand(1)); 0
351 if (!Op0 || !Op1) 0
352 return std::optional{}; 0
353 if (I->getOpcode() == Instruction::Add) 0
354 return std::optional{*Op0 + *Op1}; 0
355 if (I->getOpcode() == Instruction::Mul) 0
356 return std::optional{*Op0 * *Op1}; 0
357 if (I->getOpcode() == Instruction::Shl) 0
358 return std::optional{*Op0 << *Op1}; 0
359 if (I->getOpcode() == Instruction::Or) 0
360 return std::optional{*Op0 | *Op1}; 0
361 } ----
362 return std::optional{}; 0
363 } ----
364 ----
365 // Return true if I is an Or instruction that is equivalent to an add, due to ----
366 // the operands having no common bits set. ----
367 static bool isAddLikeOr(Instruction *I, const DataLayout &DL) { 0
368 return I->getOpcode() == Instruction::Or && 0
369 haveNoCommonBitsSet(I->getOperand(0), I->getOperand(1), DL); 0
370 } ----

372 std::pair ----
373 MVEGatherScatterLowering::getVarAndConst(Value *Inst, int TypeScale) { 0
374 std::pair ReturnFalse = 0
375 std::pair(nullptr, 0); ----
376 // At this point, the instruction we're looking at must be an add or an ----
377 // add-like-or. ----
378 Instruction *Add = dyn_cast(Inst); 0
379 if (Add == nullptr || 0
380 (Add->getOpcode() != Instruction::Add && !isAddLikeOr(Add, *DL))) 0
381 return ReturnFalse; 0
382 ----
383 Value *Summand; ----
384 std::optional Const; 0
385 // Find out which operand the value that is increased is ----
386 if ((Const = getIfConst(Add->getOperand(0)))) 0
387 Summand = Add->getOperand(1); 0
388 else if ((Const = getIfConst(Add->getOperand(1)))) 0
389 Summand = Add->getOperand(0); 0
390 else ----
391 return ReturnFalse; 0
392 ----
393 // Check that the constant is small enough for an incrementing gather ----
394 int64_t Immediate = *Const << TypeScale; 0
395 if (Immediate > 512 || Immediate < -512 || Immediate % 4 != 0) 0
396 return ReturnFalse; 0
397 ----
398 return std::pair(Summand, Immediate); 0
399 } ----

401 Instruction *MVEGatherScatterLowering::lowerGather(IntrinsicInst *I) { 0
402 using namespace PatternMatch; ----
403 LLVM_DEBUG(dbgs() << "masked gathers: checking transform preconditions\n" 0
404 << *I << "\n"); ----
405 ----
406 // @llvm.masked.gather.*(Ptrs, alignment, Mask, Src0) ----
407 // Attempt to turn the masked gather in I into a MVE intrinsic ----
408 // Potentially optimising the addressing modes as we do so. ----
409 auto *Ty = cast(I->getType()); 0
410 Value *Ptr = I->getArgOperand(0); 0
411 Align Alignment = cast(I->getArgOperand(1))->getAlignValue(); 0
412 Value *Mask = I->getArgOperand(2); 0
413 Value *PassThru = I->getArgOperand(3); 0
414 ----
415 if (!isLegalTypeAndAlignment(Ty->getNumElements(), Ty->getScalarSizeInBits(), 0
416 Alignment)) ----
417 return nullptr; 0
418 lookThroughBitcast(Ptr); 0
419 assert(Ptr->getType()->isVectorTy() && "Unexpected pointer type"); 0
420 ----
421 IRBuilder<> Builder(I->getContext()); 0
422 Builder.SetInsertPoint(I); 0
423 Builder.SetCurrentDebugLocation(I->getDebugLoc()); 0
424 ----
425 Instruction *Root = I; 0
426 ----
427 Instruction *Load = tryCreateIncrementingGatScat(I, Ptr, Builder); 0
428 if (!Load) 0
429 Load = tryCreateMaskedGatherOffset(I, Ptr, Root, Builder); 0
430 if (!Load) 0
431 Load = tryCreateMaskedGatherBase(I, Ptr, Builder); 0
432 if (!Load) 0
433 return nullptr; 0
434 ----
435 if (!isa(PassThru) && !match(PassThru, m_Zero())) { 0
436 LLVM_DEBUG(dbgs() << "masked gathers: found non-trivial passthru - " 0
437 << "creating select\n"); ----
438 Load = SelectInst::Create(Mask, Load, PassThru); 0
439 Builder.Insert(Load); 0
440 } ----
441 ----
442 Root->replaceAllUsesWith(Load); 0
443 Root->eraseFromParent(); 0
444 if (Root != I) 0
445 // If this was an extending gather, we need to get rid of the sext/zext ----
446 // sext/zext as well as of the gather itself ----
447 I->eraseFromParent(); 0
448 ----
449 LLVM_DEBUG(dbgs() << "masked gathers: successfully built masked gather\n" 0
450 << *Load << "\n"); ----
451 return Load; 0
452 } 0
453 ----
454 Instruction *MVEGatherScatterLowering::tryCreateMaskedGatherBase( 0
455 IntrinsicInst *I, Value *Ptr, IRBuilder<> &Builder, int64_t Increment) { ----
456 using namespace PatternMatch; ----
457 auto *Ty = cast(I->getType()); 0
458 LLVM_DEBUG(dbgs() << "masked gathers: loading from vector of pointers\n"); 0
459 if (Ty->getNumElements() != 4 || Ty->getScalarSizeInBits() != 32) 0
460 // Can't build an intrinsic for this ----
461 return nullptr; 0
462 Value *Mask = I->getArgOperand(2); 0
463 if (match(Mask, m_One())) 0
464 return Builder.CreateIntrinsic(Intrinsic::arm_mve_vldr_gather_base, 0
465 {Ty, Ptr->getType()}, 0
466 {Ptr, Builder.getInt32(Increment)}); 0
467 else ----
468 return Builder.CreateIntrinsic( 0
469 Intrinsic::arm_mve_vldr_gather_base_predicated, ----
470 {Ty, Ptr->getType(), Mask->getType()}, 0
471 {Ptr, Builder.getInt32(Increment), Mask}); 0
472 } ----
473 ----
474 Instruction *MVEGatherScatterLowering::tryCreateMaskedGatherBaseWB( 0
475 IntrinsicInst *I, Value *Ptr, IRBuilder<> &Builder, int64_t Increment) { ----
476 using namespace PatternMatch; ----
477 auto *Ty = cast(I->getType()); 0
478 LLVM_DEBUG(dbgs() << "masked gathers: loading from vector of pointers with " 0
479 << "writeback\n"); ----
480 if (Ty->getNumElements() != 4 || Ty->getScalarSizeInBits() != 32) 0
481 // Can't build an intrinsic for this ----
482 return nullptr; 0
483 Value *Mask = I->getArgOperand(2); 0
484 if (match(Mask, m_One())) 0
485 return Builder.CreateIntrinsic(Intrinsic::arm_mve_vldr_gather_base_wb, 0
486 {Ty, Ptr->getType()}, 0
487 {Ptr, Builder.getInt32(Increment)}); 0
488 else ----
489 return Builder.CreateIntrinsic( 0
490 Intrinsic::arm_mve_vldr_gather_base_wb_predicated, ----
491 {Ty, Ptr->getType(), Mask->getType()}, 0
492 {Ptr, Builder.getInt32(Increment), Mask}); 0
493 } ----
494 ----
495 Instruction *MVEGatherScatterLowering::tryCreateMaskedGatherOffset( 0
496 IntrinsicInst *I, Value *Ptr, Instruction *&Root, IRBuilder<> &Builder) { ----
497 using namespace PatternMatch; ----
498 ----
499 Type *MemoryTy = I->getType(); 0
500 Type *ResultTy = MemoryTy; 0
501 ----
502 unsigned Unsigned = 1; 0
503 // The size of the gather was already checked in isLegalTypeAndAlignment; ----
504 // if it was not a full vector width an appropriate extend should follow. ----
505 auto *Extend = Root; 0
506 bool TruncResult = false; 0
507 if (MemoryTy->getPrimitiveSizeInBits() < 128) { 0
508 if (I->hasOneUse()) { 0
509 // If the gather has a single extend of the correct type, use an extending ----
510 // gather and replace the ext. In which case the correct root to replace ----
511 // is not the CallInst itself, but the instruction which extends it. ----
512 Instruction* User = cast(*I->users().begin()); 0
513 if (isa(User) && 0
514 User->getType()->getPrimitiveSizeInBits() == 128) { 0
515 LLVM_DEBUG(dbgs() << "masked gathers: Incorporating extend: " 0
516 << *User << "\n"); ----
517 Extend = User; 0
518 ResultTy = User->getType(); 0
519 Unsigned = 0; 0
520 } else if (isa(User) && 0
521 User->getType()->getPrimitiveSizeInBits() == 128) { 0
522 LLVM_DEBUG(dbgs() << "masked gathers: Incorporating extend: " 0
523 << *ResultTy << "\n"); ----
524 Extend = User; 0
525 ResultTy = User->getType(); 0
526 } ----
527 } ----
528 ----
529 // If an extend hasn't been found and the type is an integer, create an ----
530 // extending gather and truncate back to the original type. ----
531 if (ResultTy->getPrimitiveSizeInBits() < 128 && 0
532 ResultTy->isIntOrIntVectorTy()) { 0
533 ResultTy = ResultTy->getWithNewBitWidth( 0
534 128 / cast(ResultTy)->getNumElements()); 0
535 TruncResult = true; 0
536 LLVM_DEBUG(dbgs() << "masked gathers: Small input type, truncing to: " 0
537 << *ResultTy << "\n"); ----
538 } ----
539 ----
540 // The final size of the gather must be a full vector width ----
541 if (ResultTy->getPrimitiveSizeInBits() != 128) { 0
542 LLVM_DEBUG(dbgs() << "masked gathers: Extend needed but not provided " 0
543 "from the correct type. Expanding\n"); ----
544 return nullptr; 0
545 } ----
546 } ----
547 ----
548 Value *Offsets; ----
549 int Scale; ----
550 Value *BasePtr = decomposePtr( 0
551 Ptr, Offsets, Scale, cast(ResultTy), MemoryTy, Builder); ----
552 if (!BasePtr) 0
553 return nullptr; 0
554 ----
555 Root = Extend; 0
556 Value *Mask = I->getArgOperand(2); 0
557 Instruction *Load = nullptr; 0
558 if (!match(Mask, m_One())) 0
559 Load = Builder.CreateIntrinsic( 0
560 Intrinsic::arm_mve_vldr_gather_offset_predicated, ----
561 {ResultTy, BasePtr->getType(), Offsets->getType(), Mask->getType()}, 0
562 {BasePtr, Offsets, Builder.getInt32(MemoryTy->getScalarSizeInBits()), 0
563 Builder.getInt32(Scale), Builder.getInt32(Unsigned), Mask}); 0
564 else ----
565 Load = Builder.CreateIntrinsic( 0
566 Intrinsic::arm_mve_vldr_gather_offset, ----
567 {ResultTy, BasePtr->getType(), Offsets->getType()}, 0
568 {BasePtr, Offsets, Builder.getInt32(MemoryTy->getScalarSizeInBits()), 0
569 Builder.getInt32(Scale), Builder.getInt32(Unsigned)}); 0
570 ----
571 if (TruncResult) { 0
572 Load = TruncInst::Create(Instruction::Trunc, Load, MemoryTy); 0
573 Builder.Insert(Load); 0
574 } ----
575 return Load; 0
576 } ----
577 ----
578 Instruction *MVEGatherScatterLowering::lowerScatter(IntrinsicInst *I) { 0
579 using namespace PatternMatch; ----
580 LLVM_DEBUG(dbgs() << "masked scatters: checking transform preconditions\n" 0
581 << *I << "\n"); ----
582 ----
583 // @llvm.masked.scatter.*(data, ptrs, alignment, mask) ----
584 // Attempt to turn the masked scatter in I into a MVE intrinsic ----
585 // Potentially optimising the addressing modes as we do so. ----
586 Value *Input = I->getArgOperand(0); 0
587 Value *Ptr = I->getArgOperand(1); 0
588 Align Alignment = cast(I->getArgOperand(2))->getAlignValue(); 0
589 auto *Ty = cast(Input->getType()); 0
590 ----
591 if (!isLegalTypeAndAlignment(Ty->getNumElements(), Ty->getScalarSizeInBits(), 0
592 Alignment)) ----
593 return nullptr; 0
594 ----
595 lookThroughBitcast(Ptr); 0
596 assert(Ptr->getType()->isVectorTy() && "Unexpected pointer type"); 0
597 ----
598 IRBuilder<> Builder(I->getContext()); 0
599 Builder.SetInsertPoint(I); 0
600 Builder.SetCurrentDebugLocation(I->getDebugLoc()); 0
601 ----
602 Instruction *Store = tryCreateIncrementingGatScat(I, Ptr, Builder); 0
603 if (!Store) 0
604 Store = tryCreateMaskedScatterOffset(I, Ptr, Builder); 0
605 if (!Store) 0
606 Store = tryCreateMaskedScatterBase(I, Ptr, Builder); 0
607 if (!Store) 0
608 return nullptr; 0
609 ----
610 LLVM_DEBUG(dbgs() << "masked scatters: successfully built masked scatter\n" 0
611 << *Store << "\n"); ----
612 I->eraseFromParent(); 0
613 return Store; 0
614 } 0
615 ----
616 Instruction *MVEGatherScatterLowering::tryCreateMaskedScatterBase( 0
617 IntrinsicInst *I, Value *Ptr, IRBuilder<> &Builder, int64_t Increment) { ----
618 using namespace PatternMatch; ----
619 Value *Input = I->getArgOperand(0); 0
620 auto *Ty = cast(Input->getType()); 0
621 // Only QR variants allow truncating ----
622 if (!(Ty->getNumElements() == 4 && Ty->getScalarSizeInBits() == 32)) { 0
623 // Can't build an intrinsic for this ----
624 return nullptr; 0
625 } ----
626 Value *Mask = I->getArgOperand(3); 0
627 // int_arm_mve_vstr_scatter_base(_predicated) addr, offset, data(, mask) ----
628 LLVM_DEBUG(dbgs() << "masked scatters: storing to a vector of pointers\n"); 0
629 if (match(Mask, m_One())) 0
630 return Builder.CreateIntrinsic(Intrinsic::arm_mve_vstr_scatter_base, 0
631 {Ptr->getType(), Input->getType()}, 0
632 {Ptr, Builder.getInt32(Increment), Input}); 0
633 else ----
634 return Builder.CreateIntrinsic( 0
635 Intrinsic::arm_mve_vstr_scatter_base_predicated, ----
636 {Ptr->getType(), Input->getType(), Mask->getType()}, 0
637 {Ptr, Builder.getInt32(Increment), Input, Mask}); 0
638 } ----
639 ----
640 Instruction *MVEGatherScatterLowering::tryCreateMaskedScatterBaseWB( 0
641 IntrinsicInst *I, Value *Ptr, IRBuilder<> &Builder, int64_t Increment) { ----
642 using namespace PatternMatch; ----
643 Value *Input = I->getArgOperand(0); 0
644 auto *Ty = cast(Input->getType()); 0
645 LLVM_DEBUG(dbgs() << "masked scatters: storing to a vector of pointers " 0
646 << "with writeback\n"); ----
647 if (Ty->getNumElements() != 4 || Ty->getScalarSizeInBits() != 32) 0
648 // Can't build an intrinsic for this ----
649 return nullptr; 0
650 Value *Mask = I->getArgOperand(3); 0
651 if (match(Mask, m_One())) 0
652 return Builder.CreateIntrinsic(Intrinsic::arm_mve_vstr_scatter_base_wb, 0
653 {Ptr->getType(), Input->getType()}, 0
654 {Ptr, Builder.getInt32(Increment), Input}); 0
655 else ----
656 return Builder.CreateIntrinsic( 0
657 Intrinsic::arm_mve_vstr_scatter_base_wb_predicated, ----
658 {Ptr->getType(), Input->getType(), Mask->getType()}, 0
659 {Ptr, Builder.getInt32(Increment), Input, Mask}); 0
660 } ----
661 ----
662 Instruction *MVEGatherScatterLowering::tryCreateMaskedScatterOffset( 0
663 IntrinsicInst *I, Value *Ptr, IRBuilder<> &Builder) { ----
664 using namespace PatternMatch; ----
665 Value *Input = I->getArgOperand(0); 0
666 Value *Mask = I->getArgOperand(3); 0
667 Type *InputTy = Input->getType(); 0
668 Type *MemoryTy = InputTy; 0
669 ----
670 LLVM_DEBUG(dbgs() << "masked scatters: getelementpointer found. Storing" 0
671 << " to base + vector of offsets\n"); ----
672 // If the input has been truncated, try to integrate that trunc into the ----
673 // scatter instruction (we don't care about alignment here) ----
674 if (TruncInst *Trunc = dyn_cast(Input)) { 0
675 Value *PreTrunc = Trunc->getOperand(0); 0
676 Type *PreTruncTy = PreTrunc->getType(); 0
677 if (PreTruncTy->getPrimitiveSizeInBits() == 128) { 0
678 Input = PreTrunc; 0
679 InputTy = PreTruncTy; 0
680 } ----
681 } ----
682 bool ExtendInput = false; 0
683 if (InputTy->getPrimitiveSizeInBits() < 128 && 0
684 InputTy->isIntOrIntVectorTy()) { 0
685 // If we can't find a trunc to incorporate into the instruction, create an ----
686 // implicit one with a zext, so that we can still create a scatter. We know ----
687 // that the input type is 4x/8x/16x and of type i8/i16/i32, so any type ----
688 // smaller than 128 bits will divide evenly into a 128bit vector. ----
689 InputTy = InputTy->getWithNewBitWidth( 0
690 128 / cast(InputTy)->getNumElements()); 0
691 ExtendInput = true; 0
692 LLVM_DEBUG(dbgs() << "masked scatters: Small input type, will extend:\n" 0
693 << *Input << "\n"); ----
694 } ----
695 if (InputTy->getPrimitiveSizeInBits() != 128) { 0
696 LLVM_DEBUG(dbgs() << "masked scatters: cannot create scatters for " 0
697 "non-standard input types. Expanding.\n"); ----
698 return nullptr; 0
699 } ----
700 ----
701 Value *Offsets; ----
702 int Scale; ----
703 Value *BasePtr = decomposePtr( 0
704 Ptr, Offsets, Scale, cast(InputTy), MemoryTy, Builder); ----
705 if (!BasePtr) 0
706 return nullptr; 0
707 ----
708 if (ExtendInput) 0
709 Input = Builder.CreateZExt(Input, InputTy); 0
710 if (!match(Mask, m_One())) 0
711 return Builder.CreateIntrinsic( 0
712 Intrinsic::arm_mve_vstr_scatter_offset_predicated, ----
713 {BasePtr->getType(), Offsets->getType(), Input->getType(), 0
714 Mask->getType()}, 0
715 {BasePtr, Offsets, Input, ----
716 Builder.getInt32(MemoryTy->getScalarSizeInBits()), 0
717 Builder.getInt32(Scale), Mask}); 0
718 else ----
719 return Builder.CreateIntrinsic( 0
720 Intrinsic::arm_mve_vstr_scatter_offset, ----
721 {BasePtr->getType(), Offsets->getType(), Input->getType()}, 0
722 {BasePtr, Offsets, Input, ----
723 Builder.getInt32(MemoryTy->getScalarSizeInBits()), 0
724 Builder.getInt32(Scale)}); 0
725 } ----
726 ----
727 Instruction *MVEGatherScatterLowering::tryCreateIncrementingGatScat( 0
728 IntrinsicInst *I, Value *Ptr, IRBuilder<> &Builder) { ----
729 FixedVectorType *Ty; ----
730 if (I->getIntrinsicID() == Intrinsic::masked_gather) 0
731 Ty = cast(I->getType()); 0
732 else ----
733 Ty = cast(I->getArgOperand(0)->getType()); 0
734 ----
735 // Incrementing gathers only exist for v4i32 ----
736 if (Ty->getNumElements() != 4 || Ty->getScalarSizeInBits() != 32) 0
737 return nullptr; 0
738 // Incrementing gathers are not beneficial outside of a loop ----
739 Loop *L = LI->getLoopFor(I->getParent()); 0
740 if (L == nullptr) 0
741 return nullptr; 0
742 ----
743 // Decompose the GEP into Base and Offsets ----
744 GetElementPtrInst *GEP = dyn_cast(Ptr); 0
745 Value *Offsets; ----
746 Value *BasePtr = decomposeGEP(Offsets, Ty, GEP, Builder); 0
747 if (!BasePtr) 0
748 return nullptr; 0
749 ----
750 LLVM_DEBUG(dbgs() << "masked gathers/scatters: trying to build incrementing " 0
751 "wb gather/scatter\n"); ----
752 ----
753 // The gep was in charge of making sure the offsets are scaled correctly ----
754 // - calculate that factor so it can be applied by hand ----
755 int TypeScale = ----
756 computeScale(DL->getTypeSizeInBits(GEP->getOperand(0)->getType()), 0
757 DL->getTypeSizeInBits(GEP->getType()) / 0
758 cast(GEP->getType())->getNumElements()); 0
759 if (TypeScale == -1) 0
760 return nullptr; 0
761 ----
762 if (GEP->hasOneUse()) { 0
763 // Only in this case do we want to build a wb gather, because the wb will ----
764 // change the phi which does affect other users of the gep (which will still ----
765 // be using the phi in the old way) ----
766 if (auto *Load = tryCreateIncrementingWBGatScat(I, BasePtr, Offsets, 0
767 TypeScale, Builder)) ----
768 return Load; 0
769 } ----
770 ----
771 LLVM_DEBUG(dbgs() << "masked gathers/scatters: trying to build incrementing " 0
772 "non-wb gather/scatter\n"); ----
773 ----
774 std::pair Add = getVarAndConst(Offsets, TypeScale); 0
775 if (Add.first == nullptr) 0
776 return nullptr; 0
777 Value *OffsetsIncoming = Add.first; 0
778 int64_t Immediate = Add.second; 0
779 ----
780 // Make sure the offsets are scaled correctly ----
781 Instruction *ScaledOffsets = BinaryOperator::Create( 0
782 Instruction::Shl, OffsetsIncoming, ----
783 Builder.CreateVectorSplat(Ty->getNumElements(), Builder.getInt32(TypeScale)), 0
784 "ScaledIndex", I); ----
785 // Add the base to the offsets ----
786 OffsetsIncoming = BinaryOperator::Create( 0
787 Instruction::Add, ScaledOffsets, ----
788 Builder.CreateVectorSplat( ----
789 Ty->getNumElements(), ----
790 Builder.CreatePtrToInt( ----
791 BasePtr, ----
792 cast(ScaledOffsets->getType())->getElementType())), ----
793 "StartIndex", I); ----
794 ----
795 if (I->getIntrinsicID() == Intrinsic::masked_gather) 0
796 return tryCreateMaskedGatherBase(I, OffsetsIncoming, Builder, Immediate); 0
797 else ----
798 return tryCreateMaskedScatterBase(I, OffsetsIncoming, Builder, Immediate); 0
799 } ----
800 ----
801 Instruction *MVEGatherScatterLowering::tryCreateIncrementingWBGatScat( 0
802 IntrinsicInst *I, Value *BasePtr, Value *Offsets, unsigned TypeScale, ----
803 IRBuilder<> &Builder) { ----
804 // Check whether this gather's offset is incremented by a constant - if so, ----
805 // and the load is of the right type, we can merge this into a QI gather ----
806 Loop *L = LI->getLoopFor(I->getParent()); 0
807 // Offsets that are worth merging into this instruction will be incremented ----
808 // by a constant, thus we're looking for an add of a phi and a constant ----
809 PHINode *Phi = dyn_cast(Offsets); 0
810 if (Phi == nullptr || Phi->getNumIncomingValues() != 2 || 0
811 Phi->getParent() != L->getHeader() || Phi->getNumUses() != 2) 0
812 // No phi means no IV to write back to; if there is a phi, we expect it ----
813 // to have exactly two incoming values; the only phis we are interested in ----
814 // will be loop IV's and have exactly two uses, one in their increment and ----
815 // one in the gather's gep ----
816 return nullptr; 0
817 ----
818 unsigned IncrementIndex = ----
819 Phi->getIncomingBlock(0) == L->getLoopLatch() ? 0 : 1; 0
820 // Look through the phi to the phi increment ----
821 Offsets = Phi->getIncomingValue(IncrementIndex); 0
822 ----
823 std::pair Add = getVarAndConst(Offsets, TypeScale); 0
824 if (Add.first == nullptr) 0
825 return nullptr; 0
826 Value *OffsetsIncoming = Add.first; 0
827 int64_t Immediate = Add.second; 0
828 if (OffsetsIncoming != Phi) 0
829 // Then the increment we are looking at is not an increment of the ----
830 // induction variable, and we don't want to do a writeback ----
831 return nullptr; 0
832 ----
833 Builder.SetInsertPoint(&Phi->getIncomingBlock(1 - IncrementIndex)->back()); 0
834 unsigned NumElems = ----
835 cast(OffsetsIncoming->getType())->getNumElements(); 0
836 ----
837 // Make sure the offsets are scaled correctly ----
838 Instruction *ScaledOffsets = BinaryOperator::Create( 0
839 Instruction::Shl, Phi->getIncomingValue(1 - IncrementIndex), ----
840 Builder.CreateVectorSplat(NumElems, Builder.getInt32(TypeScale)), 0
841 "ScaledIndex", &Phi->getIncomingBlock(1 - IncrementIndex)->back()); 0
842 // Add the base to the offsets ----
843 OffsetsIncoming = BinaryOperator::Create( 0
844 Instruction::Add, ScaledOffsets, ----
845 Builder.CreateVectorSplat( ----
846 NumElems, ----
847 Builder.CreatePtrToInt( ----
848 BasePtr, ----
849 cast(ScaledOffsets->getType())->getElementType())), ----
850 "StartIndex", &Phi->getIncomingBlock(1 - IncrementIndex)->back()); 0
851 // The gather is pre-incrementing ----
852 OffsetsIncoming = BinaryOperator::Create( 0
853 Instruction::Sub, OffsetsIncoming, ----
854 Builder.CreateVectorSplat(NumElems, Builder.getInt32(Immediate)), 0
855 "PreIncrementStartIndex", ----
856 &Phi->getIncomingBlock(1 - IncrementIndex)->back()); 0
857 Phi->setIncomingValue(1 - IncrementIndex, OffsetsIncoming); 0
858 ----
859 Builder.SetInsertPoint(I); 0
860 ----
861 Instruction *EndResult; ----
862 Instruction *NewInduction; ----
863 if (I->getIntrinsicID() == Intrinsic::masked_gather) { 0
864 // Build the incrementing gather ----
865 Value *Load = tryCreateMaskedGatherBaseWB(I, Phi, Builder, Immediate); 0
866 // One value to be handed to whoever uses the gather, one is the loop ----
867 // increment ----
868 EndResult = ExtractValueInst::Create(Load, 0, "Gather"); 0
869 NewInduction = ExtractValueInst::Create(Load, 1, "GatherIncrement"); 0
870 Builder.Insert(EndResult); 0
871 Builder.Insert(NewInduction); 0
872 } else { ----
873 // Build the incrementing scatter ----
874 EndResult = NewInduction = 0
875 tryCreateMaskedScatterBaseWB(I, Phi, Builder, Immediate); 0
876 } ----
877 Instruction *AddInst = cast(Offsets); 0
878 AddInst->replaceAllUsesWith(NewInduction); 0
879 AddInst->eraseFromParent(); 0
880 Phi->setIncomingValue(IncrementIndex, NewInduction); 0
881 ----
882 return EndResult; 0
883 } ----
884 ----
885 void MVEGatherScatterLowering::pushOutAdd(PHINode *&Phi, 0
886 Value *OffsSecondOperand, ----
887 unsigned StartIndex) { ----
888 LLVM_DEBUG(dbgs() << "masked gathers/scatters: optimising add instruction\n"); 0
889 Instruction *InsertionPoint = ----
890 &cast(Phi->getIncomingBlock(StartIndex)->back()); 0
891 // Initialize the phi with a vector that contains a sum of the constants ----
892 Instruction *NewIndex = BinaryOperator::Create( 0
893 Instruction::Add, Phi->getIncomingValue(StartIndex), OffsSecondOperand, ----
894 "PushedOutAdd", InsertionPoint); ----
895 unsigned IncrementIndex = StartIndex == 0 ? 1 : 0; 0
896 ----
897 // Order such that start index comes first (this reduces mov's) ----
898 Phi->addIncoming(NewIndex, Phi->getIncomingBlock(StartIndex)); 0
899 Phi->addIncoming(Phi->getIncomingValue(IncrementIndex), 0
900 Phi->getIncomingBlock(IncrementIndex)); ----
901 Phi->removeIncomingValue(IncrementIndex); 0
902 Phi->removeIncomingValue(StartIndex); 0
903 } 0
904 ----
905 void MVEGatherScatterLowering::pushOutMulShl(unsigned Opcode, PHINode *&Phi, 0
906 Value *IncrementPerRound, ----
907 Value *OffsSecondOperand, ----
908 unsigned LoopIncrement, ----
909 IRBuilder<> &Builder) { ----
910 LLVM_DEBUG(dbgs() << "masked gathers/scatters: optimising mul instruction\n"); 0
911 ----
912 // Create a new scalar add outside of the loop and transform it to a splat ----
913 // by which loop variable can be incremented ----
914 Instruction *InsertionPoint = &cast( 0
915 Phi->getIncomingBlock(LoopIncrement == 1 ? 0 : 1)->back()); 0
916 ----
917 // Create a new index ----
918 Value *StartIndex = ----
919 BinaryOperator::Create((Instruction::BinaryOps)Opcode, 0
920 Phi->getIncomingValue(LoopIncrement == 1 ? 0 : 1), 0
921 OffsSecondOperand, "PushedOutMul", InsertionPoint); ----
922 ----
923 Instruction *Product = ----
924 BinaryOperator::Create((Instruction::BinaryOps)Opcode, IncrementPerRound, 0
925 OffsSecondOperand, "Product", InsertionPoint); ----
926 // Increment NewIndex by Product instead of the multiplication ----
927 Instruction *NewIncrement = BinaryOperator::Create( 0
928 Instruction::Add, Phi, Product, "IncrementPushedOutMul", ----
929 cast(Phi->getIncomingBlock(LoopIncrement)->back()) 0
930 .getPrevNode()); ----
931 ----
932 Phi->addIncoming(StartIndex, 0
933 Phi->getIncomingBlock(LoopIncrement == 1 ? 0 : 1)); 0
934 Phi->addIncoming(NewIncrement, Phi->getIncomingBlock(LoopIncrement)); 0
935 Phi->removeIncomingValue((unsigned)0); 0
936 Phi->removeIncomingValue((unsigned)0); 0
937 } 0
938 ----
939 // Check whether all usages of this instruction are as offsets of ----
940 // gathers/scatters or simple arithmetics only used by gathers/scatters ----
941 static bool hasAllGatScatUsers(Instruction *I, const DataLayout &DL) { 0
942 if (I->hasNUses(0)) { 0
943 return false; 0
944 } ----
945 bool Gatscat = true; 0
946 for (User *U : I->users()) { 0
947 if (!isa(U)) 0
948 return false; 0
949 if (isa(U) || 0
950 isGatherScatter(dyn_cast(U))) { 0
951 return Gatscat; 0
952 } else { ----
953 unsigned OpCode = cast(U)->getOpcode(); 0
954 if ((OpCode == Instruction::Add || OpCode == Instruction::Mul || 0
955 OpCode == Instruction::Shl || 0
956 isAddLikeOr(cast(U), DL)) && 0
957 hasAllGatScatUsers(cast(U), DL)) { 0
958 continue; 0
959 } ----
960 return false; 0
961 } ----
962 } ----
963 return Gatscat; 0
964 } ----
965 ----
966 bool MVEGatherScatterLowering::optimiseOffsets(Value *Offsets, BasicBlock *BB, 0
967 LoopInfo *LI) { ----
968 LLVM_DEBUG(dbgs() << "masked gathers/scatters: trying to optimize: " 0
969 << *Offsets << "\n"); ----
970 // Optimise the addresses of gathers/scatters by moving invariant ----
971 // calculations out of the loop ----
972 if (!isa(Offsets)) 0
973 return false; 0
974 Instruction *Offs = cast(Offsets); 0
975 if (Offs->getOpcode() != Instruction::Add && !isAddLikeOr(Offs, *DL) && 0
976 Offs->getOpcode() != Instruction::Mul && 0
977 Offs->getOpcode() != Instruction::Shl) 0
978 return false; 0
979 Loop *L = LI->getLoopFor(BB); 0
980 if (L == nullptr) 0
981 return false; 0
982 if (!Offs->hasOneUse()) { 0
983 if (!hasAllGatScatUsers(Offs, *DL)) 0
984 return false; 0
985 } ----
986 ----
987 // Find out which, if any, operand of the instruction ----
988 // is a phi node ----
989 PHINode *Phi; ----
990 int OffsSecondOp; ----
991 if (isa(Offs->getOperand(0))) { 0
992 Phi = cast(Offs->getOperand(0)); 0
993 OffsSecondOp = 1; 0
994 } else if (isa(Offs->getOperand(1))) { 0
995 Phi = cast(Offs->getOperand(1)); 0
996 OffsSecondOp = 0; 0
997 } else { ----
998 bool Changed = false; 0
999 if (isa(Offs->getOperand(0)) && 0
1000 L->contains(cast(Offs->getOperand(0)))) 0
1001 Changed |= optimiseOffsets(Offs->getOperand(0), BB, LI); 0
1002 if (isa(Offs->getOperand(1)) && 0
1003 L->contains(cast(Offs->getOperand(1)))) 0
1004 Changed |= optimiseOffsets(Offs->getOperand(1), BB, LI); 0
1005 if (!Changed) 0
1006 return false; 0
1007 if (isa(Offs->getOperand(0))) { 0
1008 Phi = cast(Offs->getOperand(0)); 0
1009 OffsSecondOp = 1; 0
1010 } else if (isa(Offs->getOperand(1))) { 0
1011 Phi = cast(Offs->getOperand(1)); 0
1012 OffsSecondOp = 0; 0
1013 } else { ----
1014 return false; 0
1015 } ----
1016 } ----
1017 // A phi node we want to perform this function on should be from the ----
1018 // loop header. ----
1019 if (Phi->getParent() != L->getHeader()) 0
1020 return false; 0
1021 ----
1022 // We're looking for a simple add recurrence. ----
1023 BinaryOperator *IncInstruction; ----
1024 Value *Start, *IncrementPerRound; ----
1025 if (!matchSimpleRecurrence(Phi, IncInstruction, Start, IncrementPerRound) || 0
1026 IncInstruction->getOpcode() != Instruction::Add) 0
1027 return false; 0
1028 ----
1029 int IncrementingBlock = Phi->getIncomingValue(0) == IncInstruction ? 0 : 1; 0
1030 ----
1031 // Get the value that is added to/multiplied with the phi ----
1032 Value *OffsSecondOperand = Offs->getOperand(OffsSecondOp); 0
1033 ----
1034 if (IncrementPerRound->getType() != OffsSecondOperand->getType() || 0
1035 !L->isLoopInvariant(OffsSecondOperand)) 0
1036 // Something has gone wrong, abort ----
1037 return false; 0
1038 ----
1039 // Only proceed if the increment per round is a constant or an instruction ----
1040 // which does not originate from within the loop ----
1041 if (!isa(IncrementPerRound) && 0
1042 !(isa(IncrementPerRound) && 0
1043 !L->contains(cast(IncrementPerRound)))) 0
1044 return false; 0
1045 ----
1046 // If the phi is not used by anything else, we can just adapt it when ----
1047 // replacing the instruction; if it is, we'll have to duplicate it ----
1048 PHINode *NewPhi; ----
1049 if (Phi->getNumUses() == 2) { 0
1050 // No other users -> reuse existing phi (One user is the instruction ----
1051 // we're looking at, the other is the phi increment) ----
1052 if (IncInstruction->getNumUses() != 1) { 0
1053 // If the incrementing instruction does have more users than ----
1054 // our phi, we need to copy it ----
1055 IncInstruction = BinaryOperator::Create( 0
1056 Instruction::BinaryOps(IncInstruction->getOpcode()), Phi, ----
1057 IncrementPerRound, "LoopIncrement", IncInstruction); ----
1058 Phi->setIncomingValue(IncrementingBlock, IncInstruction); 0
1059 } ----
1060 NewPhi = Phi; 0
1061 } else { ----
1062 // There are other users -> create a new phi ----
1063 NewPhi = PHINode::Create(Phi->getType(), 2, "NewPhi", Phi); 0
1064 // Copy the incoming values of the old phi ----
1065 NewPhi->addIncoming(Phi->getIncomingValue(IncrementingBlock == 1 ? 0 : 1), 0
1066 Phi->getIncomingBlock(IncrementingBlock == 1 ? 0 : 1)); 0
1067 IncInstruction = BinaryOperator::Create( 0
1068 Instruction::BinaryOps(IncInstruction->getOpcode()), NewPhi, ----
1069 IncrementPerRound, "LoopIncrement", IncInstruction); ----
1070 NewPhi->addIncoming(IncInstruction, 0
1071 Phi->getIncomingBlock(IncrementingBlock)); ----
1072 IncrementingBlock = 1; 0
1073 } ----
1074 ----
1075 IRBuilder<> Builder(BB->getContext()); 0
1076 Builder.SetInsertPoint(Phi); 0
1077 Builder.SetCurrentDebugLocation(Offs->getDebugLoc()); 0
1078 ----
1079 switch (Offs->getOpcode()) { 0
1080 case Instruction::Add: 0
1081 case Instruction::Or: ----
1082 pushOutAdd(NewPhi, OffsSecondOperand, IncrementingBlock == 1 ? 0 : 1); 0
1083 break; 0
1084 case Instruction::Mul: 0
1085 case Instruction::Shl: ----
1086 pushOutMulShl(Offs->getOpcode(), NewPhi, IncrementPerRound, 0
1087 OffsSecondOperand, IncrementingBlock, Builder); ----
1088 break; 0
1089 default: 0
1090 return false; 0
1091 } ----
1092 LLVM_DEBUG(dbgs() << "masked gathers/scatters: simplified loop variable " 0
1093 << "add/mul\n"); ----
1094 ----
1095 // The instruction has now been "absorbed" into the phi value ----
1096 Offs->replaceAllUsesWith(NewPhi); 0
1097 if (Offs->hasNUses(0)) 0
1098 Offs->eraseFromParent(); 0
1099 // Clean up the old increment in case it's unused because we built a new ----
1100 // one ----
1101 if (IncInstruction->hasNUses(0)) 0
1102 IncInstruction->eraseFromParent(); 0
1103 ----
1104 return true; 0
1105 } 0
1106 ----
1107 static Value *CheckAndCreateOffsetAdd(Value *X, unsigned ScaleX, Value *Y, 0
1108 unsigned ScaleY, IRBuilder<> &Builder) { ----
1109 // Splat the non-vector value to a vector of the given type - if the value is ----
1110 // a constant (and its value isn't too big), we can even use this opportunity ----
1111 // to scale it to the size of the vector elements ----
1112 auto FixSummands = [&Builder](FixedVectorType *&VT, Value *&NonVectorVal) { 0
1113 ConstantInt *Const; ----
1114 if ((Const = dyn_cast(NonVectorVal)) && 0
1115 VT->getElementType() != NonVectorVal->getType()) { 0
1116 unsigned TargetElemSize = VT->getElementType()->getPrimitiveSizeInBits(); 0
1117 uint64_t N = Const->getZExtValue(); 0
1118 if (N < (unsigned)(1 << (TargetElemSize - 1))) { 0
1119 NonVectorVal = Builder.CreateVectorSplat( 0
1120 VT->getNumElements(), Builder.getIntN(TargetElemSize, N)); 0
1121 return; 0
1122 } ----
1123 } ----
1124 NonVectorVal = 0
1125 Builder.CreateVectorSplat(VT->getNumElements(), NonVectorVal); 0
1126 }; 0
1127 ----
1128 FixedVectorType *XElType = dyn_cast(X->getType()); 0
1129 FixedVectorType *YElType = dyn_cast(Y->getType()); 0
1130 // If one of X, Y is not a vector, we have to splat it in order ----
1131 // to add the two of them. ----
1132 if (XElType && !YElType) { 0
1133 FixSummands(XElType, Y); 0
1134 YElType = cast(Y->getType()); 0
1135 } else if (YElType && !XElType) { 0
1136 FixSummands(YElType, X); 0
1137 XElType = cast(X->getType()); 0
1138 } ----
1139 assert(XElType && YElType && "Unknown vector types"); 0
1140 // Check that the summands are of compatible types ----
1141 if (XElType != YElType) { 0
1142 LLVM_DEBUG(dbgs() << "masked gathers/scatters: incompatible gep offsets\n"); 0
1143 return nullptr; 0
1144 } ----
1145 ----
1146 if (XElType->getElementType()->getScalarSizeInBits() != 32) { 0
1147 // Check that by adding the vectors we do not accidentally ----
1148 // create an overflow ----
1149 Constant *ConstX = dyn_cast(X); 0
1150 Constant *ConstY = dyn_cast(Y); 0
1151 if (!ConstX || !ConstY) 0
1152 return nullptr; 0
1153 unsigned TargetElemSize = 128 / XElType->getNumElements(); 0
1154 for (unsigned i = 0; i < XElType->getNumElements(); i++) { 0
1155 ConstantInt *ConstXEl = ----
1156 dyn_cast(ConstX->getAggregateElement(i)); 0
1157 ConstantInt *ConstYEl = ----
1158 dyn_cast(ConstY->getAggregateElement(i)); 0
1159 if (!ConstXEl || !ConstYEl || 0
1160 ConstXEl->getZExtValue() * ScaleX + 0
1161 ConstYEl->getZExtValue() * ScaleY >= 0
1162 (unsigned)(1 << (TargetElemSize - 1))) 0
1163 return nullptr; 0
1164 } ----
1165 } ----
1166 ----
1167 Value *XScale = Builder.CreateVectorSplat( 0
1168 XElType->getNumElements(), ----
1169 Builder.getIntN(XElType->getScalarSizeInBits(), ScaleX)); 0
1170 Value *YScale = Builder.CreateVectorSplat( 0
1171 YElType->getNumElements(), ----
1172 Builder.getIntN(YElType->getScalarSizeInBits(), ScaleY)); 0
1173 Value *Add = Builder.CreateAdd(Builder.CreateMul(X, XScale), 0
1174 Builder.CreateMul(Y, YScale)); ----
1175 ----
1176 if (checkOffsetSize(Add, XElType->getNumElements())) 0
1177 return Add; 0
1178 else ----
1179 return nullptr; 0
1180 } ----

1182 Value *MVEGatherScatterLowering::foldGEP(GetElementPtrInst *GEP, 0
1183 Value *&Offsets, unsigned &Scale, ----
1184 IRBuilder<> &Builder) { ----
1185 Value *GEPPtr = GEP->getPointerOperand(); 0
1186 Offsets = GEP->getOperand(1); 0
1187 Scale = DL->getTypeAllocSize(GEP->getSourceElementType()); 0
1188 // We only merge geps with constant offsets, because only for those ----
1189 // we can make sure that we do not cause an overflow ----
1190 if (GEP->getNumIndices() != 1 || !isa(Offsets)) 0
1191 return nullptr; 0
1192 if (GetElementPtrInst *BaseGEP = dyn_cast(GEPPtr)) { 0
1193 // Merge the two geps into one ----
1194 Value *BaseBasePtr = foldGEP(BaseGEP, Offsets, Scale, Builder); 0
1195 if (!BaseBasePtr) 0
1196 return nullptr; 0
1197 Offsets = CheckAndCreateOffsetAdd( 0
1198 Offsets, Scale, GEP->getOperand(1), ----
1199 DL->getTypeAllocSize(GEP->getSourceElementType()), Builder); 0
1200 if (Offsets == nullptr) 0
1201 return nullptr; 0
1202 Scale = 1; // Scale is always an i8 at this point. 0
1203 return BaseBasePtr; 0
1204 } ----
1205 return GEPPtr; 0
1206 } ----

1208 bool MVEGatherScatterLowering::optimiseAddress(Value *Address, BasicBlock *BB, 0
1209 LoopInfo *LI) { ----
1210 GetElementPtrInst *GEP = dyn_cast(Address); 0
1211 if (!GEP) 0
1212 return false; 0
1213 bool Changed = false; 0
1214 if (GEP->hasOneUse() && isa(GEP->getPointerOperand())) { 0
1215 IRBuilder<> Builder(GEP->getContext()); 0
1216 Builder.SetInsertPoint(GEP); 0
1217 Builder.SetCurrentDebugLocation(GEP->getDebugLoc()); 0
1218 Value *Offsets; ----
1219 unsigned Scale; ----
1220 Value *Base = foldGEP(GEP, Offsets, Scale, Builder); 0
1221 // We only want to merge the geps if there is a real chance that they can be ----
1222 // used by an MVE gather; thus the offset has to have the correct size ----
1223 // (always i32 if it is not of vector type) and the base has to be a ----
1224 // pointer. ----
1225 if (Offsets && Base && Base != GEP) { 0
1226 assert(Scale == 1 && "Expected to fold GEP to a scale of 1"); 0
1227 Type *BaseTy = Builder.getInt8PtrTy(); 0
1228 if (auto *VecTy = dyn_cast(Base->getType())) 0

1231 Builder.getInt8Ty(), Builder.CreateBitCast(Base, BaseTy), Offsets, 0
1232 "gep.merged", GEP); ----
1233 LLVM_DEBUG(dbgs() << "Folded GEP: " << *GEP 0
1234 << "\n new : " << *NewAddress << "\n"); ----
1235 GEP->replaceAllUsesWith( 0
1236 Builder.CreateBitCast(NewAddress, GEP->getType())); ----
1237 GEP = NewAddress; 0
1238 Changed = true; 0
1239 } ----
1240 } 0
1241 Changed |= optimiseOffsets(GEP->getOperand(1), GEP->getParent(), LI); 0

1245 bool MVEGatherScatterLowering::runOnFunction(Function &F) { 0
1246 if (!EnableMaskedGatherScatters) 0
1247 return false; 0
1248 auto &TPC = getAnalysis(); 0
1249 auto &TM = TPC.getTM(); 0
1250 auto *ST = &TM.getSubtarget(F); 0
1251 if (!ST->hasMVEIntegerOps()) 0
1252 return false; 0
1253 LI = &getAnalysis().getLoopInfo(); 0
1254 DL = &F.getParent()->getDataLayout(); 0
1255 SmallVector Gathers; 0
1256 SmallVector Scatters; 0
1257 ----
1258 bool Changed = false; 0
1259 ----
1260 for (BasicBlock &BB : F) { 0
1261 Changed |= SimplifyInstructionsInBlock(&BB); 0
1262 ----
1263 for (Instruction &I : BB) { 0
1264 IntrinsicInst *II = dyn_cast(&I); 0
1265 if (II && II->getIntrinsicID() == Intrinsic::masked_gather && 0
1266 isa(II->getType())) { 0
1267 Gathers.push_back(II); 0
1268 Changed |= optimiseAddress(II->getArgOperand(0), II->getParent(), LI); 0
1269 } else if (II && II->getIntrinsicID() == Intrinsic::masked_scatter && 0
1270 isa(II->getArgOperand(0)->getType())) { 0
1271 Scatters.push_back(II); 0
1272 Changed |= optimiseAddress(II->getArgOperand(1), II->getParent(), LI); 0
1273 } ----
1274 } ----
1275 } ----
1276 for (unsigned i = 0; i < Gathers.size(); i++) { 0
1277 IntrinsicInst *I = Gathers[i]; 0
1278 Instruction *L = lowerGather(I); 0
1279 if (L == nullptr) 0
1280 continue; 0
1281 ----
1282 // Get rid of any now dead instructions ----
1283 SimplifyInstructionsInBlock(L->getParent()); 0
1284 Changed = true; 0
1285 } ----
1286 ----
1287 for (unsigned i = 0; i < Scatters.size(); i++) { 0
1288 IntrinsicInst *I = Scatters[i]; 0
1289 Instruction *S = lowerScatter(I); 0
1290 if (S == nullptr) 0
1291 continue; 0
1292 ----
1293 // Get rid of any now dead instructions ----
1294 SimplifyInstructionsInBlock(S->getParent()); 0
1295 Changed = true; 0
1296 } ----
1297 return Changed; 0
1298 } 0
